        if(oRemoveAds.indexOf('trb_ad_300x250_1_/') != -1 && true) {
          let label = document.getElementById('label_hp_0')
          label && label.classList.add('hddn')
          adFlag = false
        }
      }
      if(adFlag) {
        
          //FetchBids for all ads
          if (((!DeviceDetection.isDesktopSize() && true) || (DeviceDetection.isDesktopSize() && true)) && (true && window.apstag) && ((true && window.headertag) || (false && window.PWT))) {
            let params = {
              id: 'hp_0',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.chicagotribune/hp',
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true
            }
            if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
              trb.data.page.ads.vendor = trb.data.page.ads.vendor || {}
              trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams = trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams || {}
            }
            const dimensions = !'[[300, 250]]'.length ? null : JSON.parse('[[300, 250]]'),
              sizemapDimensions = !''.length ? null : JSON.parse('')
            if (sizemapDimensions) {
              const mapping = DFPHelpers.prepareSizeMaps(dimensions, sizemapDimensions).mapping
              const parsedMapping = DFPHelpers.parseSizeMappings(mapping)
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_0'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : parsedMapping}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(parsedMapping, params)
            } else {
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_0'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : dimensions}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(dimensions, params)
            }
          }
          
            if (trb.data.ads.optimera) {
              if (!window.oPageUnload) {
                oAv.push("trb_ad_300x250_1_/");
                oVa["trb_ad_300x250_1_/"] = ["NULL"];
              } else {
                oPageUnload('trb_ad_300x250_1_/', true);
              }
            }
          
          function loadAd() {
            dfpService.appendAd({
              id: 'hp_0',
              optimeraId: 'trb_ad_300x250_1_/',
              adType: 'cube',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.chicagotribune/hp',
              displayMobile: true,
              displayDesktop: true,
              isOOP: false,
              is5x1: false,
              dimensionsString: '[[300, 250]]',
              sizemapString: '',
              sizemapRefresh: 'false',
              refreshOnPhotoChange: false,
              adRefreshInterval: 0,
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true,
              loadImmediately: true
            }, false, true)
          }
          loadAd();
        
      }
    })()
  </script> </div> <div class=" wrapper clearfix col pb-automated col-desktop-6 col-tablet-6 col-mobile-6 pb-feature pb-layout-item pb-f-list-recommender" data-pb-name="Recommender"
